{"step_index":1996,"source":"MODEL","type":"PLANNER_RESPONSE","status":"DONE","created_at":"2026-05-03T11:15:18Z","content":"坑在这儿：`.map_err(|e| e.to_string())??`。\n`spawn_blocking` 返回的是 `Result<Result<T, E>, JoinError>`，所以 `await` 之后拿到的也是这个。\n接个 `.map_err(|e| e.to_string())`，它就变成了 `Result<Result<T, E>, String>`。\n第一个 `?` 剥开外层，剩下 `Result<T, E>`。\n第二个 `?` 剥开里层，但这有个前提：`E` 必须能转成函数的返回错误类型。对大多数 Tauri 命令来说，这个类型是 `String`。\n如果 `E` 本身就是 `String`，按说没啥问题。\n\n但要是 `E` 的定义不够明确，编译器可能就撂挑子了。\n我得查查 `PdfReadFacade::get_page_preview` 到底返回的是个啥。\n\n去 `engine.rs` 翻翻 `get_page_preview` 的定义。\n\n---\n\n","tool_calls":[{"name":"view_file","args":{"AbsolutePath":"\"e:\\\\chain\\\\pdf-viewer-standalone\\\\src-tauri\\\\src\\\\infrastructure\\\\multimedia\\\\pdf\\\\engine.rs\"","EndLine":"250","StartLine":"180","toolAction":"\"Checking get_page_preview.\"","toolSummary":"\"split 10-52 check engine preview 2\""}}]}
